:* D O M I N I Q U E ~~
It's from the inadequacy of a person to be concerned only with personal gratification & satisfaction.
Do you suffer from face-addiction? Or do you seek beauty in the imperfections of a person?
You may know what you are looking for in a partner, but are you aware of what YOU have to offer?
Allah likens spouses to a garment thus know & understand it consists of imperfections.
Men & Women are different: understand this for effective communication & know differences to cohabit.
Marriage is a partnership not a competition between two people: it should establish an equilibrium.
Falling in love is easy, sustaining that requires effort & for it to be coupled with mercy.
We marry to create a comfortable space for individual & collective growth both emotionally & spiritually.
Too often we forget that marriage is a union between two personalities, not a correctional institution.
Finding a partner is only the very beginning, sustaining the marriage is what defines it.
